(group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) manages offsets with state tracked in ClassicGroupState CoordinatorLoaderImpl (core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/CoordinatorLoaderImpl.scala) loads offsets from __consumer_offsets during startup.\\n\\n10. **Admin API Support**: Multiple handlers support admin operations on offsets including ListConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler, AlterConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler, and DeleteConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler.\\n\\n11. **Modern Group Types**: Support for consumer groups (ConsumerGroup), share groups (ShareGroup), and streams groups (StreamsGroup) with their respective offset management in the modern group protocol.\\n\\nAll offset data is persisted in the Kafka cluster's special __consumer_offsets topic using record types defined by OffsetCommitKey/OffsetCommitValue and processed through the GroupCoordinator's runtime, which uses timeline-based It works with GroupCoordinatorService (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java) and GroupCoordinatorShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java) to process offset commits and fetches.\\n\\n3. **OffsetMetadataManager**: This class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java) is the core manager for all offset operations, handling both request processing and offset data storage in the __consumer_offsets topic through the timeline data structures.\\n\\n4. **OffsetFetch Request Handling**: The OffsetFetcher (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/OffsetFetcher.java) handles client-side offset fetching. The server-side processing occurs in KafkaApis.scala (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaApis.scala) which routes OffsetFetch requests to the GroupCoordinator.\\n\\n5. **OffsetCommit Request Handling**: The CommitRequestManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java) handles client-side offset commits. The server-side OffsetMetadataManager processes these requests and stores them in __consumer_offsets using the CoordinatorPartitionWriter (core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/CoordinatorPartitionWriter.scala).\\n\\n6. **Offset Expiry and Compaction**: The OffsetExpirationCondition (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationCondition.java) and OffsetExpirationConditionImpl (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationConditionImpl.java) implement offset expiration logic, while compaction of the __consumer_offsets topic is handled through the coordinator's built-in compaction using cleanup policy.\\n\\n7. **ClassicGroup Support**: For legacy consumer groups, ClassicGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) manages offsets with state tracked in ClassicGroupState (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java).\\n\\n8. **Transactional Offsets**: TxnOffsetCommitRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/TxnOffsetCommitRequest.java) and TxnOffsetCommitResponse handle offsets within transactions.\\n\\n9. **Offset Loading**: The CoordinatorLoaderImpl (core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/CoordinatorLoaderImpl.scala) loads offsets from __consumer_offsets during startup.\\n\\n10. **Admin API Support**: Multiple handlers support admin operations on offsets including ListConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler, AlterConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler, and DeleteConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler.\\n\\n11. **Modern Group Types**: Support for consumer groups (ConsumerGroup), share groups (ShareGroup), and streams groups (StreamsGroup) with their respective offset management in the modern group protocol.\\n\\nAll offset data is persisted in the Kafka cluster's special __consumer_offsets topic using record types defined by OffsetCommitKey/OffsetCommitValue and processed through the GroupCoordinator's runtime, which uses timeline-based snapshots for efficient storage and retrieval.\"\n}","stderr":"","interrupted":false,"isImage":false,"noOutputExpected":false}}
